name:X‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçu‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçm‚Äçe‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçz‚Äçh‚Äçi‚Äçl‚Äçv
info:Superior King
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:18 Reviews
rating:4.3
posted:Posted May 1, 2024
msg:Arrived in Linyi at around 13:00 in the afternoon. Check-in was fast and all was matched according to the requirements of advance notes. The front desk staff was warm and polite. They gave the baby a small gift and explained breakfast and other matters to me. The service was very good. There is also a local tourist map at the front desk, which is very practical.
When I first arrived in this city, I found that the roads were very clean, there were many bridges, and the main road was close to the Yi River, which was particularly beautiful. The location of the hotel is also very good. Opposite is Phoenix Square, which is particularly suitable for elderly people to walk along the road.
The room has a good view, with sofa chairs, desks, and pillows. There is a mobile phone holder on the desktop, the bathroom is relatively small, and the bathtub is large. The wireless network is too slow and the overall decoration is slightly old. When I came back in the evening, I was given fruit and the bed guard was also added. The night view around the hotel is beautiful, the light show, and Xinlangya are not far away, and the night market is not crowded and very lively.
In the evening, the baby went to the swimming pool for a while. There were basically no people, and the swimming ring was not allowed. The baby's father accompanied him to swim for an hour. The water is relatively clean. Although the swimming pool is not too big, the small number of people really adds points. I only saw a beautiful woman exercising in the gym.
There were many people at breakfast but it was not crowded. The waiter would take the initiative to greet and help get food. The dishes were quite rich. There were two kinds of braised quail eggs in the noodle stall, and the pancakes with Sanzi were very unique. There was a children's playground in the restaurant, with slides, ocean balls, etc., which the children especially liked. Check-out was also relatively fast.
A small episode was that I asked the hotel to help with freezing water, but I waited for half an hour to check out the next day and didn't get it back. It was delivered when I was leaving. Another thing was that two of the three rooms were given fruit plates, but the other one was not. Also, the network was really bad in the room, but everything else was OK.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Superior Room - River-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Couples
info:20 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted April 23, 2024
msg:I was passing by Linyi and it was my first time to Linyi. I stopped for a while and found this hotel ranked first in luxury hotels on Ctrip. I followed the navigation and when I first arrived at the hotel and saw the exterior of the hotel, I felt that I was in the wrong place. It didn't seem to be luxurious at all. The glass curtain wall on the outside of the hotel really needed to be cleaned. It looked quite old during the day. When I drove to the underground parking lot, I felt cold in my heart. The entrance looked shabby. I walked in and felt it was okay. The lights were bright and the parking spaces were neat. But the hygiene was worrying and the smell was unpleasant. There is an elevator from the basement to the hotel lobby, and it is very convenient to go directly to the floor. Since we checked in on Saturday, there were a lot of people in the lobby and it was a bit chaotic, but the front desk service was still very enthusiastic. They called in advance to ask about the guests' needs before checking in, and helped us upgrade when we checked in (although we didn't ask for it). We still stayed in the previous room type. The room area is large enough and the design is reasonable. The furniture is a little old. It's because of the age. It's quite satisfactory. It's worth praising that the view outside the floor-to-ceiling window is great, which makes people feel happy. The bed and pillow are very comfortable and can wash away fatigue. The sound insulation of the room is really bad. The voices of talking and calling in the corridor can be heard clearly, which needs to be improved. The hotel has an excellent location, which is convenient for travel. It is very close to the old and new Langya. I just want to say that Langya will be boring except for the background of lights. Maybe I don't like these light pollutions, but I still prefer the original charm. Finally, I must mention the waiter and restaurant manager Wang at the buffet on the first floor of the hotel. The service is very warm and thoughtful. It really feels like home. I give you a thumbs up!

msg:1. Location & transportation:
The location of the hotel is very good. You can see the convergence of the Yi River, the Yi River and the Liuqing River, Linyi's version of the Bund.
There is a green walking trail nearby, and you can reach Phoenix Square along the Jiukong Bridge, as well as the water bus terminal.
It's about 10-15 minutes' drive from the city center and the airport, making it suitable for business trips.

2. Catering & Services:
I received a call from the customer care manager in advance and thanked me for the upgrade to a river view room. I saw the pleasing "Y", Phoenix Square, and TV Tower in the room.
The room card is unique, the rooms are clean, the breakfast is rich in variety, and there are local specialties such as glutinous rice dumplings. The ingredients for the buffet dinner are fresh and worth trying.

3. Facilities & Equipment:
The decoration is a bit old but the facilities are well maintained and the bedding is very comfortable. Spare parts are also OK.

Overall, the stay was a pleasant experience and the service was very warm!

msg:Pullman Linyi Lushang is considered to be a relatively large landmark hotel in Linyi. It is close to the government affairs center, cultural center and scenic spots. It is not only the first choice for business people, but also a good place for tourists to check in on vacation.
The supporting facilities in the bedroom are complete and perfect, such as sofas, office desks and chairs, and central air-conditioning, which are enough reasons to choose this hotel as a place to stay for business trips. Because the hotel has a high floor and is located in the bustling area of Linyi City Center, the viewing field is very wide. From the guest room, you can have a bird's-eye view of the confluence of three rivers in Linyi and the scenery of the TV Tower. The supporting facilities are very suitable for business people, but also suitable for tourism and vacation. Sure enough, it is both business and vacation.
Hotel rooms are divided into smoking rooms and non-smoking rooms. The hotel front desk will allocate rooms according to whether you smoke or not. This kind of humanized design is worth mentioning, after all, many business people will smoke cigarettes more or less.
The hotel is quite sophisticated in terms of Feng Shui, and the arcs are used between the floors. It uses arcs to create circular trajectories, thereby generating centripetal force and alleviating the conflict between floors, which has the effect of balancing the aura and adding aesthetic depth to the building.
